Source Code

These source-code files were derived originally from the scan from MIT's Dibner Institute's now-discontinued website titled "History of Recent Science and Technology", which in turn was originally created by Gary Neff, though his high-quality scans were unfortunately reduced in legibility when presented online. The markings on the front of the printout imply that it was the original AGC developer Norm Brodeur's copy. A scan by Ron Burkey has superceded it, made from a more-legible copy from the collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. The source code was transcribed from those images by Ron Burkey. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	ASSEMBLE REVISION 249 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS BY NASA 2021111-041
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

000002,000002:                                                                                                  #  Copyright:    Public domain.
000003,000003:                                                                                                  #  Filename:     MAIN.agc
000004,000004:                                                                                                  #  Purpose:      Part of the source code for Colossus, build 249.
000005,000005:                                                                                                  #                It is part of the source code for the Command Module's (CM)
000006,000006:                                                                                                  #                Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), possibly for Apollo 8 and 9.
000007,000007:                                                                                                  #  Assembler:    yaYUL
000008,000008:                                                                                                  #  Contact:      Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
000009,000009:                                                                                                  #  Website:      www.ibiblio.org/apollo
000010,000010:                                                                                                  #  Mod history:  04/30/03 RSB.   Created using the Luminary131 file of the 
000011,000011:                                                                                                  #                                same name as a model.
000012,000012:                                                                                                  #                08/02/04 RSB    Resumed Colossus development.
000013,000013:                                                                                                  #                08/22/04 RSB    Filled in all of the page numbers for the
000014,000014:                                                                                                  #                                individual include-files.
000015,000015: 
000016,000016:                                                                                                  #  The contents of the "Colossus249" files, in general, are transcribed 
000017,000017:                                                                                                  #  from a scanned document obtained from MIT's website,
000018,000018:                                                                                                  #  http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1701.pdf.  I'd like to note
000019,000019:                                                                                                  #  that the character-set of the line-printer used must not have completely
000020,000020:                                                                                                  #  agreed with the one the developers had in mind, so I've interpreted various
000021,000021:                                                                                                  #  wacky symbols appearing in the print as follows:
000022,000022: 
000023,000023:                                                                                                  #        Print                           Interpretation
000024,000024:                                                                                                  #        -----                           --------------
000025,000025:                                                                                                  #        plus-minus                            <
000026,000026:                                                                                                  #        lower-case Greek delta                >
000027,000027:                                                                                                  #        lower-case Greek nu              | (sometimes)
000028,000028:                                                                                                  #        strange lower-case d                  &
000029,000029:                                                                                                  #        trailing '                            :
000030,000030:                                                                                                  #        other                           still uninterpreted
000031,000031: 
000032,000032:                                                                                                  #  Notations on the scanned document read, in part:
000033,000033: 
000034,000034:                                                                                                  #        Assemble revision 249 of AGC program Colossus by NASA
000035,000035:                                                                                                  #        2021111-041.  October 28, 1968.  
000036,000036: 
000037,000037:                                                                                                  #        This AGC program shall also be referred to as
000038,000038:                                                                                                  #                                Colossus 1A
000039,000039: 
000040,000040:                                                                                                  #        Prepared by
000041,000041:                                                                                                  #                        Massachusetts Institute of Technology
000042,000042:                                                                                                  #                        75 Cambridge Parkway
000043,000043:                                                                                                  #                        Cambridge, Massachusetts
000044,000044:                                                                                                  #        under NASA contract NAS 9-4065.
000045,000045: 
000046,000046:                                                                                                  #  Refer directly to the online document mentioned above for further information.
000047,000047:                                                                                                  #  Please report any errors (relative to 1701.pdf) to info@sandroid.org.
000048,000048: 
000049,000049:                                                                                                  #  This file is a little different from the other Colossus249 files I'm providing, 
000050,000050:                                                                                                  #  in that it doesn't represent anything that appears directly in the original source.  
000051,000051:                                                                                                  #  What I (RSB) have done for organizational purposes is to split the huge monolithic
000052,000052:                                                                                                  #  source code into smaller, more manageable chunks--i.e., into individual source 
000053,000053:                                                                                                  #  files.  Those files are rejoined within this file as "includes".  It just makes
000054,000054:                                                                                                  #  it a little easier to work with.  The code chunks correspond to natural divisions
000055,000055:                                                                                                  #  into sub-programs.  In fact, these divisions are more-or-less specified by
000056,000056:                                                                                                  #  the source code itself.  Refer to the "SUBROUTINE CALLS" at the
000057,000057:                                                                                                  #  very beginning of the file ASSEMBLY_AND_OPERATION_INFORMATION.agc.
000058,000058: 
000059,000059:                                                                                                  #  It may be reasonably asked why tens of thousands of lines of source are joined by
000060,000060:                                                                                                  #  means of inclusion, rather than simply assembling the source files individually and
000061,000061:                                                                                                  #  then linking them to form the executable.  The answer is that the original 
000062,000062:                                                                                                  #  development team had no linker.  The builds were monolithic just like this.
000063,000063:                                                                                                  #  There was a big emphasis on reusability of the code in the original project, 
000064,000064:                                                                                                  #  apparently, but this reusability took the form of inserting your deck of 
000065,000065:                                                                                                  #  punch-cards at the appropriate position in somebody else's deck of punch-cards.
000066,000066:                                                                                                  #  So, indeed, the method of file-inclusion is a very fair representation of the 
000067,000067:                                                                                                  #  methods used in the original development ... with the improvement, of course,
000068,000068:                                                                                                  #  that you no longer have to worry about dropping the card deck.  On the other hand, 
000069,000069:                                                                                                  #  I wasn't there at the time, so I may have no idea what I'm talking about.
000070,000070: 
000071,000071:                                                                                                  #  Finally, note that the original Apollo AGC assembler (called "YUL") is no longer 
000072,000072:                                                                                                  #  available (as far as I can tell).  The replacement assembler yaYUL accepts 
000073,000073:                                                                                                  #  a slightly different format for the source code from what YUL accepted, so the 
000074,000074:                                                                                                  #  source code has been targeted for assembly with yaYUL.
000075,000075: 
000076,000076:                                                                                                  #  What follows is simply a bunch of file-includes for the individual code chunks.
000077,000077:                                                                                                  #  I've marked the page numbers vs. the original scanned listing (1701.pdf) to 
000078,000078:                                                                                                  #  make proof-reading easier.  Besides, the scanned listing contains a lot of
000079,000079:                                                                                                  #  interesting tables (cross-referenced to page numbers) created by YUL, 
000080,000080:                                                                                                  #  but not duplicated by yaYUL, so it's still valuable even if the source-files
000081,000081:                                                                                                  #  listed below are in hand.
000082,000082: 
000083,000083:                                                                                                  #  pp. 1-2 contain no code/comments.
